{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01VcXdk5SZt1gtkNcxcn7XPZ","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→\"\"\"Pipeline executor -- generic step sequencer with retry, gates, and parallel dispatch.\n     2→\n     3→Composition-via-callable design: consumers (sprint, roadmap) inject their own\n     4→StepRunner and callbacks. The executor handles step ordering, retry logic,\n     5→parallel dispatch, and state management.\n     6→\n     7→NFR-007: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n     8→\"\"\"\n     9→\n    10→from __future__ import annotations\n    11→\n    12→import logging\n    13→import threading\n    14→from datetime import datetime, timezone\n    15→from typing import Callable, Protocol\n    16→\n    17→from .gates import gate_passed\n    18→from .models import GateMode, PipelineConfig, Step, StepResult, StepStatus\n    19→from .trailing_gate import TrailingGateRunner\n    20→\n    21→_log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.executor\")\n    22→\n    23→\n    24→class StepRunner(Protocol):\n    25→    \"\"\"Callable that executes a single step's subprocess and returns a result.\n    26→\n    27→    The runner is responsible for:\n    28→    - Launching the claude -p subprocess\n    29→    - Waiting for completion (with timeout enforcement)\n    30→    - Returning a StepResult with appropriate status\n    31→\n    32→    The runner is NOT responsible for:\n    33→    - Retry logic (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    34→    - Gate checking (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    35→    - Step ordering (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    36→    \"\"\"\n    37→\n    38→    def __call__(\n    39→        self,\n    40→        step: Step,\n    41→        config: PipelineConfig,\n    42→        cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    43→    ) -> StepResult: ...\n    44→\n    45→\n    46→def execute_pipeline(\n    47→    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    48→    config: PipelineConfig,\n    49→    run_step: StepRunner,\n    50→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    51→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    52→    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    53→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n    54→    trailing_runner: TrailingGateRunner | None = None,\n    55→) -> list[StepResult]:\n    56→    \"\"\"Generic pipeline executor.\n    57→\n    58→    Processes steps in order. Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    59→    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    60→    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n    61→\n    62→    For each step:\n    63→    1. Call on_step_start(step)\n    64→    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    65→    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n    66→       - BLOCKING mode: evaluate synchronously, halt on failure\n    67→       - TRAILING mode (grace_period > 0): submit to TrailingGateRunner,\n    68→         continue execution; sync point at end collects results\n    69→    4. If gate fails and attempts < retry_limit: retry (go to 2)\n    70→    5. If gate fails and attempts exhausted: HALT\n    71→    6. Call on_step_complete(step, result)\n    72→    7. Call on_state_update(updated_state_dict)\n    73→\n    74→    For parallel step groups:\n    75→    - All steps in the group run concurrently via _run_parallel_steps()\n    76→    - If any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled\n    77→    - All results from the group must be PASS before proceeding\n    78→\n    79→    Returns list of all StepResults (one per step, flattened).\n    80→    \"\"\"\n    81→    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n    82→    # Create trailing runner if grace_period > 0 and none provided\n    83→    _trailing = trailing_runner\n    84→    if _trailing is None and config.grace_period > 0:\n    85→        _trailing = TrailingGateRunner()\n    86→\n    87→    for entry in steps:\n    88→        if cancel_check():\n    89→            break\n    90→\n    91→        if isinstance(entry, list):\n    92→            # Parallel step group\n    93→            for s in entry:\n    94→                on_step_start(s)\n    95→\n    96→            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n    97→            all_results.extend(group_results)\n    98→\n    99→            for r in group_results:\n   100→                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n   101→\n   102→            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n   103→\n   104→            # If any step in the group failed, halt\n   105→            if any(r.status != StepStatus.PASS for r in group_results):\n   106→                break\n   107→        else:\n   108→            # Sequential step -- branch on gate_mode\n   109→            result = _execute_single_step(\n   110→                entry, config, run_step, cancel_check,\n   111→                on_step_start, on_step_complete,\n   112→                trailing_runner=_trailing,\n   113→            )\n   114→            all_results.append(result)\n   115→            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n   116→\n   117→            if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n   118→                break\n   119→\n   120→    # Sync point: collect all trailing gate results at end of pipeline\n   121→    if _trailing is not None:\n   122→        trailing_results = _trailing.wait_for_pending(\n   123→            timeout=max(30.0, float(config.grace_period))\n   124→        )\n   125→        for tr in trailing_results:\n   126→            if not tr.passed:\n   127→                _log.warning(\n   128→                    \"Trailing gate failed for step '%s': %s\",\n   129→                    tr.step_id,\n   130→                    tr.failure_reason,\n   131→                )\n   132→\n   133→    return all_results\n   134→\n   135→\n   136→def _execute_single_step(\n   137→    step: Step,\n   138→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   139→    run_step: StepRunner,\n   140→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   141→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n   142→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n   143→    trailing_runner: TrailingGateRunner | None = None,\n   144→) -> StepResult:\n   145→    \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic and gate checking.\n   146→\n   147→    Gate mode branching:\n   148→    - BLOCKING (default): gate evaluates synchronously before proceeding\n   149→    - TRAILING (grace_period > 0): gate submitted to TrailingGateRunner,\n   150→      step returns PASS immediately and execution continues\n   151→    - grace_period == 0 forces BLOCKING regardless of gate_mode\n   152→    \"\"\"\n   153→    on_step_start(step)\n   154→    max_attempts = step.retry_limit + 1  # retry_limit=1 means 2 attempts total\n   155→\n   156→    # Determine effective gate mode\n   157→    effective_mode = step.gate_mode\n   158→    if config.grace_period == 0:\n   159→        effective_mode = GateMode.BLOCKING\n   160→\n   161→    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n   162→        if cancel_check():\n   163→            now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   164→            result = StepResult(\n   165→                step=step,\n   166→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   167→                attempt=attempt,\n   168→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   169→                started_at=now,\n   170→                finished_at=now,\n   171→            )\n   172→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   173→            return result\n   174→\n   175→        result = run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n   176→        result = StepResult(\n   177→            step=result.step,\n   178→            status=result.status,\n   179→            attempt=attempt,\n   180→            gate_failure_reason=result.gate_failure_reason,\n   181→            started_at=result.started_at,\n   182→            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n   183→        )\n   184→\n   185→        # Call on_step_start(step)\n    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n       - BLOCKING mode: evaluate synchronously, halt on failure\n       - TRAILING mode (grace_period > 0): submit to TrailingGateRunner,\n         continue execution; sync point at end collects results\n    4. Parallel step group\n            for s in entry:\n                on_step_start(s)\n\n            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n            all_results.extend(group_results)\n\n            for r in group_results:\n                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            # Gate failed\n        _log.info(\"Gate failed for step '%s' (attempt %d/%d): %s\", step.id, attempt, max_attempts, reason)\n\n        if attempt < max_attempts:\n            continue  # retry\n\n        # Exhausted retries\n        result = StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=attempt,\n            gate_failure_reason=reason,\n            started_at=result.started_at,\n            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n        )\n        on_step_complete(step, result)\n        return result\n\n    # fenced code blocks.\n    57→\n    58→    Each file is wrapped in a fenced block with a ``# <path>`` header.\n    59→    Returns an empty string when *input_paths* is empty (no-op).\n    60→    \"\"\"\n    61→    if not input_paths:\n    62→        return \"\"\n    63→\n    64→    blocks: list[str] = []\n    65→    for p in input_paths:\n    66→        content = _sanitize_output(output_file: Path) -> int:\n    72→    \"\"\"Strip conversational preamble before YAML frontmatter in a step output file.\n    73→\n    74→    Reads the file, finds the first ``^---`` line, and removes everything before\n    75→    it.  Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    76→    partial file states.\n    77→\n    78→    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    79→    with ``---`` or no frontmatter delimiter is found).\n    80→    \"\"\"\n    81→    import os\n    82→    import re\n    83→\n    84→    try:\n    85→        content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    86→    except FileNotFoundError:\n    87→        return 0\n    88→\n    89→    # Already starts with frontmatter delimiter -- nothing to strip\n    90→ 95→    if match is None:\n    96→        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n    97→        return 0\n    98→\n    99→    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n   100→    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n   101→    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   102→\n   103→    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n   104→    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n   105→    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   106→    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n   107→\n   108→    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n   109→    return preamble_bytes\n   110→\n   111→\n   112→def _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n   113→    output_file: Path,\n   114→    started_at: datetime,\n   115→    finished_at: datetime,\n   116→) -> None:\n   117→    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n   118→\n   119→    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n   120→    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n   121→    \"\"\"\n   122→    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   123→    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   124→        return\n   125→\n   126→    # Find end of frontmatter\n   127→    end_idx = 143→        + diagnostics_line\n   144→        + content[end_idx:]\n   145→    )\n   146→    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   147→\n   148→\n   149→def roadmap_run_step(\n 394→\n   395→def _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n   396→    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n   397→    failed = [r for r 521→\n   522→\n   523→def _save_state(config: RoadmapConfig, results: list[StepResult]) -> None:\n   524→    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json to output_dir via atomic tmp + os.replace().\n   525→\n \"\"\"Derive fidelity_status enum from a spec-fidelity StepResult.\n   574→\n   575→    Returns one of: 'pass', 'fail', 'skipped', 'degraded'.\n   576→    \"\"\"\n   577→    if result.status == 584→    if result.status == StepStatus.SKIPPED:\n   585→        return \"skipped\"\n   586→    if result.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT):\n   587→        return \"fail\"\n   588→ {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_01UgVy2fL97g1MMomTnApaUA","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01SNkJ8FeYihV53PgDFHSUdh","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.dev/releases/current/v2.22-RoadmapRemediate/artifacts/D-0001/notes.md","content":"# D-0001: Pipeline Foundation Review Notes\n\n## Overview\n\nReview of the existing pipeline infrastructure to confirm extension points, state schema, and patterns available for v2.22 remediate/certify steps.\n\n---\n\n## 1. execute_pipeline() Step Model\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/executor.py`\n\n### Step Sequencing\n- `execute_pipeline()` accepts `steps: list[Step | list[Step]]` -- a mixed list where:\n  - Single `Step` entries execute sequentially\n  - `list[Step]` entries execute as parallel groups (all steps in the group run concurrently via threads)\n- For each step: `on_step_start` -> `run_step()` -> gate check -> `on_step_complete` -> `on_state_update`\n- If any step fails after retry exhaustion: pipeline HALTs (no further steps execute)\n- Parallel groups: if any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled via `threading.Event`\n\n### Retry Logic\n- `retry_limit` on `Step` dataclass controls retries (retry_limit=1 means 2 total attempts)\n- Retry only happens when gate check fails; subprocess errors (non-zero exit, timeout) are terminal\n\n### Gate Evaluation\n- Two modes: `GateMode.BLOCKING` (synchronous, default) and `GateMode.TRAILING` (deferred, grace period)\n- `grace_period == 0` forces BLOCKING regardless of step's `gate_mode`\n- Trailing gates collect at sync point after all steps complete\n\n### State Save Pattern\n- `_build_state()` produces a dict with `steps`, `total`, `passed`, `failed` counts\n- Called via `on_state_update` callback after each step/group completes\n- Consumers (roadmap, sprint) provide their own `on_state_update` implementation\n\n### Extension Points\n- **StepRunner Protocol**: Any callable matching `(Step, PipelineConfig, Callable[[], bool]) -> StepResult`\n- **Callbacks**: `on_step_start`, `on_step_complete`, `on_state_update`, `cancel_check`\n- **TrailingGateRunner**: Optional trailing gate support\n\n---\n\n## 2. execute_roadmap() Extension Points\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/executor.py`\n\n### Pipeline Composition\n- `_build_steps()` constructs a 9-step pipeline (8 sequential + 1 parallel group for generate)\n- Steps: extract -> [generate-A, generate-B] -> diff -> debate -> score -> merge -> test-strategy -> spec-fidelity\n- `execute_roadmap()` is the top-level orchestrator that:\n  1. Builds steps via `_build_steps()`\n  2. Handles `--dry-run` and `--resume`\n  3. Delegates to `execute_pipeline()` with `roadmap_run_step` as the StepRunner\n  4. Saves state via `_save_state()`\n  5. Auto-invokes validation via `_auto_invoke_validate()`\n\n### Extension Points for New Steps\n- New steps (remediate, certify) can be added to the `_build_steps()` return list\n- `execute_roadmap()` already handles post-pipeline actions (validation) -- remediation can follow the same pattern\n- The interactive prompt (FR-003, FR-032) should live in `execute_roadmap()`, NOT in `execute_pipeline()`, preserving the latter's non-interactive contract\n\n### State Preservation\n- `_save_state()` preserves existing `validation` and `fidelity_status` keys across rewrites\n- New keys (e.g., `remediate`, `certify`) can be added additively without breaking backward compatibility\n\n---\n\n## 3. validate_executor.py -- ClaudeProcess Patterns\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_executor.py`\n\n### Agent Spawning Pattern\n- `validate_run_step()` mirrors `roadmap_run_step()`: builds argv, launches ClaudeProcess, waits with timeout, sanitizes output\n- Both use the same `ClaudeProcess` API with identical parameter patterns:\n  - `prompt`, `output_file`, `error_file`, `max_turns`, `model`, `permission_flag`, `timeout_seconds`, `output_format`, `extra_args`\n- Inline embedding pattern: read input files into prompt string (up to 100KB), fall back to `--file` flags for larger inputs\n\n### Multi-Agent Parallel Execution\n- `_build_multi_agent_steps()`: creates N parallel reflection steps (one per agent), then a sequential adversarial-merge step\n- The parallel group pattern is: `[reflect_steps, merge_step]` -- parallel reflections followed by sequential merge\n- **Precedent for remediation**: This is the exact pattern needed for parallel remediation agents (one per finding/file batch)\n\n### Degraded Mode Handling\n- `_write_degraded_report()`: writes a report with `validation_complete: false` when agents partially fail\n- This pattern can be reused for remediation -- partial agent failure should produce a degraded tasklist update\n\n---\n\n## 4. Gate/State Models\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n### GateCriteria Dataclass\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass GateCriteria:\n    required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]\n    min_lines: int\n    enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"\n    semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None\n```\n\n### SemanticCheck Dataclass\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass SemanticCheck:\n    name: str\n    check_fn: Callable[[str], bool]\n    failure_message: str\n```\n\n### Step Dataclass\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass Step:\n    id: str\n    prompt: str\n    output_file: Path\n    gate: Optional[GateCriteria]\n    timeout_seconds: int\n    inputs: list[Path] = field(default_factory=list)\n    retry_limit: int = 1\n    model: str = \"\"\n    gate_mode: GateMode = GateMode.BLOCKING\n```\n\n### StepStatus Enum\n- Values: PENDING, PASS, FAIL, TIMEOUT, CANCELLED, SKIPPED\n- Properties: `is_terminal` (all except PENDING), `is_success` (PASS only), `is_failure` (FAIL, TIMEOUT)\n\n### Gate Evaluation Tiers (pipeline/gates.py)\n- EXEMPT: always passes\n- LIGHT: file exists + non-empty\n- STANDARD: + min_lines + YAML frontmatter fields\n- STRICT: + semantic checks\n\n---\n\n## 5. Resume Flow\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/executor.py` (`_apply_resume`)\n\n### Resume Logic\n1. Read `.roadmap-state.json` from output_dir\n2. Check spec hash: if spec file changed since last run, force re-run of extract step\n3. For each step in pipeline order:\n   - If step has a gate: run `gate_passed()` against existing output file\n   - If gate passes: skip the step\n   - On first failing gate: include that step and all subsequent steps\n4. subprocess errors (non-zero exit, timeout) are terminal\n\n### Gate Evaluation\n- Two modes: `GateMode.BLOCKING` (synchronous, default) and `GateMode.TRAILING` (deferred, grace period)\n- `grace_period == 0` forces BLOCKING regardless of step's `gate_mode`\n- Trailing gates collect at sync point after all steps complete\n\n### State Save Pattern\n- `_build_state()` produces a dict with `steps`, `total`, `passed`, `failed` counts\n- Called via `on_state_update` callback after each step/group completes\n- Consumers (roadmap, sprint) provide their own `on_state_update` implementation\n\n### Extension Points\n- **StepRunner Protocol**: Any callable matching `(Step, PipelineConfig, Callable[[], bool]) -> StepResult`\n- **Callbacks**: `on_step_start`, `on_step_complete`, `on_state_update`, `cancel_check`\n- **TrailingGateRunner**: Optional trailing gate support\n\n---\n\n## 2. execute_roadmap() Extension Points\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/executor.py`\n\n### Pipeline Composition\n- `_build_steps()` constructs a 9-step pipeline (8 sequential + 1 parallel group for generate)\n- Steps: extract -> [generate-A, generate-B] -> diff -> debate -> score -> merge -> test-strategy -> spec-fidelity\n- `execute_roadmap()` is the top-level orchestrator that:\n  1. Builds steps via `_build_steps()`\n  2. Handles `--dry-run` and `--resume`\n  3. Delegates to `execute_pipeline()` with `roadmap_run_step` as the StepRunner\n  4. Saves state via `_save_state()`\n  5. Gate/State Models\n\n**Source**: `src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n### GateCriteria Dataclass\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass GateCriteria:\n    required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]\n    min_lines: int\n    enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"\n    semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None\n```\n\n### SemanticCheck Dataclass\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass SemanticCheck:\n    name: str\n    check_fn: Callable[[str], bool]\n    failure_message: str\n```\n\n### Step Dataclass\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass Step:\n    id: str\n    prompt: str\n    output_file: Path\n    gate: Optional[GateCriteria]\n    timeout_seconds: int\n    inputs: list[Path] = field(default_factory=list)\n    retry_limit: int = 1\n    model: str = \"\"\n    gate_mode: GateMode = GateMode.BLOCKING\n```\n\n### StepStatus Enum\n- Values: PENDING, PASS, FAIL, TIMEOUT, CANCELLED, SKIPPED\n- Properties: `is_terminal` (all except PENDING), `is_success` (PASS only), `is_failure` (FAIL, TIMEOUT)\n\n### Gate Evaluation Tiers (pipeline/gates.py)\n- EXEMPT: always passes\n- LIGHT: file exists + non-empty\n- STANDARD: + min_lines + YAML frontmatter fields\n- STRICT: + semantic checks\n\n---\n\n## 5. No conflicts detected.**\n\n### Evidence\n\n1. **SHA-256 is the established pattern** for content integrity in the pipeline:\n   - `roadmap/executor.py:529`: `hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()` for spec file hash in state\n   - `roadmap/executor.py:825`: Same pattern for resume stale-detection\n   - `audit/tool_orchestrator.py:101`: `hashlib.sha256(content.encode(\"utf-8\")).hexdigest()` for audit content deduplication\n\n2. **No SHA-256 conflicts** exist in the codebase:\n   - SHA-1 usage (`sprint/tmux.py:29`): only for short session naming hashes, non-security\n   - MD5 usage (`execution/self_correction.py:292`): only for failure ID generation, non-security\n   - Neither interferes with adopting SHA-256 for `source_report_hash`\n\n3. **Consistency with existing state schema**:\n   - `.roadmap-state.json` already stores `spec_hash` as a SHA-256 hexdigest\n   - Using the same algorithm for `source_report_hash` maintains consistency\n\n### Risk Assessment\n- **Zero risk**: SHA-256 is already the standard; this decision simply extends the existing pattern\n- **Confidence**: 98%\n\n---\n\n## Decision 3: Step Wiring -- Remediate via ClaudeProcess, Certify via execute_pipeline()\n\n### Question (OQ-003)\nShould `remediate` use `ClaudeProcess` directly or go through `execute_pipeline()`? What about `certify`?\n\n### Decision\n**Remediate uses `ClaudeProcess` directly (like `validate_run_step`). Certify uses `execute_pipeline()` (like standard roadmap steps).**\n\n### Evidence\n\n1. **Precedent: `validate_run_step` uses ClaudeProcess directly** (`validate_executor.py:77-173`):\n   - `validate_run_step()` builds its own ClaudeProcess, manages lifecycle, and returns StepResult\n   - The validate executor then passes this as the StepRunner to `execute_pipeline()`\n   - This two-tier pattern is the established approach: custom ClaudeProcess management wrapped in a StepRunner\n\n2. **Remediate needs direct ClaudeProcess control** because:\n   - Remediation agents operate on specific file batches, requiring per-finding prompt construction\n   - Each agent needs unique input context (finding details, file contents, fix guidance)\n   - The `validate_executor.py` multi-agent pattern (parallel ClaudeProcess instances) is the exact precedent\n\n3. **Certify fits the standard pipeline pattern** because:\n   - Certification is a single-pass operation: read remediated files + findings, produce a pass/fail report\n   - It follows the same shape as existing steps (prompt + inputs -> output + gate check)\n   - Using `execute_pipeline()` gives automatic retry, gate checking, and state management\n\n4. **Wiring implementation pattern**:\n   - Create `remediate_executor.py` with `remediate_run_step()` (ClaudeProcess, like `validate_run_step`)\n   - Create `certify_executor.py` or add certify steps to `_build_steps()` (execute_pipeline, like standard steps)\n   - Wire both into `execute_roadmap()` as post-validation phases\n\n### Risk Assessment\n- **Low risk**: Both patterns are already proven in the codebase\n- **Confidence**: 95%\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\n| Decision | Resolution | Confidence | Evidence Source |\n|----------|-----------|------------|-----------------|\n| OQ-001: SIGINT | Snapshot + existing ClaudeProcess signal handling | 90% | `process.py:143-184`, `executor.py:206-218` |\n| OQ-002: Hash | SHA-256 (consistent with existing) | 98% | `executor.py:529`, `tool_orchestrator.py:101` |\n| OQ-003: Step Wiring | remediate=ClaudeProcess, certify=execute_pipeline | 95% | `validate_executor.py:77-173`, `executor.py:293-392` |\n\nAll three decisions are validated against codebase evidence and locked for Phase 2 implementation.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Defines valid statuses, transitions, terminal states, and initial state assignment rules.\n\n---\n\n## State Machine\n\n```\n                  +---> FIXED    (agent remediation succeeded)\n                  |\nPENDING ----+---> FAILED   (agent remediation failed / timed out / rollback triggered)\n                  |\n                  +---> SKIPPED  (filtered out / NO_ACTION_REQUIRED / OUT_OF_SCOPE)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Status Definitions\n\n| Status | Value | Description | Terminal? |\n|--------|-------|-------------|-----------|\n| PENDING | `\"PENDING\"` | Finding parsed from validation report; awaiting remediation | No |\n| FIXED | `\"FIXED\"` | Remediation agent successfully applied fix; certify step confirms | Yes |\n| FAILED | `\"FAILED\"` | Remediation agent failed, timed out, or rollback was triggered | Yes |\n| SKIPPED | `\"SKIPPED\"` | Finding excluded from remediation by filter or classification | Yes |\n\n---\n\n## Transition Rules\n\n### Valid Transitions\n\n| From | To | Trigger | Phase |\n|------|----|---------|-------|\n| PENDING | FIXED | Agent completes successfully; output passes verification | Phase 3 (Remediation Execution) |\n| PENDING | FAILED | Agent exits non-zero, times out, or rollback is triggered | Phase 3 (Remediation Execution) |\n| PENDING | SKIPPED | Finding filtered by scope selection (option 1/2/3) | Phase 2 (Prompt & Filter) |\n| PENDING | SKIPPED | Finding classified as NO_ACTION_REQUIRED | Phase 2 (Prompt & Filter) |\n| PENDING | SKIPPED | Finding classified as OUT_OF_SCOPE | Phase 2 (Prompt & Filter) |\n\n### Invalid Transitions (Enforced)\n\n- FIXED -> any: terminal state, no further transitions\n- FAILED -> any: terminal state, no further transitions\n- SKIPPED -> any: terminal state, no further transitions\n- Any -> PENDING: initial state only, never re-assigned\n\n---\n\n## Initial State Assignment\n\n1. **Parser output**: All findings parsed from validation reports are assigned `status = PENDING`\n2. **Immediate SKIP**: During Phase 2 filtering:\n   - Findings with `agreement_category == \"NO_ACTION_REQUIRED\"` -> `SKIPPED`\n   - Findings with `agreement_category == \"OUT_OF_SCOPE\"` -> `SKIPPED`\n   - Findings outside the user's scope selection (option 1: BLOCKING only, option 2: BLOCKING+WARNING) -> `SKIPPED`\n3. **Zero-findings guard**: If 0 actionable findings remain after filtering, all findings are `SKIPPED` and pipeline proceeds to certify with stub tasklist\n\n---\n\n## Scenario Coverage\n\n### Scenario 1: Filtering (Phase 2)\n- User selects Option 1 (BLOCKING only)\n- WARNING and INFO findings -> `SKIPPED`\n- BLOCKING findings remain `PENDING` for remediation\n\n### Scenario 2: Successful Remediation (Phase 3)\n- Agent receives finding with `status = PENDING`\n- Agent modifies target files successfully\n- Output passes basic verification\n- Finding -> `FIXED`\n\n### Scenario 3: Failed Remediation (Phase 3)\n- Agent receives finding with `status = PENDING`\n- Agent exits non-zero or times out\n- Snapshot rollback triggers (`.pre-remediate` files restored)\n- Finding -> `FAILED`\n\n### Scenario 4: Rollback-Triggered Failure (Phase 3)\n- Agent modifies files but introduces errors\n- Post-remediation check detects issues\n- Rollback to `.pre-remediate` snapshot\n- Finding -> `FAILED`\n\n### Scenario 5: Skip Remediation Path (Phase 2)\n- User selects option `n` (skip remediation)\n- All PENDING findings -> remain `PENDING` (state saved as `validated-with-issues`)\n- No transition occurs; pipeline ends without remediation\n\n### Scenario 6: Zero Actionable Findings (Phase 2)\n- All findings are NO_ACTION_REQUIRED or OUT_OF_SCOPE\n- All findings -> `SKIPPED`\n- Stub tasklist generated (`actionable: 0`)\n- Pipeline proceeds to certify\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Notes\n\n### Finding Dataclass Field\n```python\nstatus: str = \"PENDING\"  # One of: PENDING, FIXED, FAILED, SKIPPED\n```\n\n### Tasklist Representation\n- `remediation-tasklist.md` records each finding with its status\n- Pre-execution: all actionable findings show `PENDING`, filtered findings show `SKIPPED`\n- Post-execution: updated in-place with `FIXED` or `FAILED` outcomes\n\n### State File Integration\n- Finding statuses are summarized in `.roadmap-state.json` under the `remediate` key\n- Summary counts: `{fixed: N, failed: N, skipped: N, total: N}`\n- Individual finding statuses stored in the tasklist artifact, not in the state file\n\n---\n\n## Alignment with Existing Pipeline Patterns\n\nThe finding lifecycle intentionally mirrors the existing `StepStatus` enum in `pipeline/models.py`:\n- `StepStatus.PASS` ~ `Finding.FIXED` (success)\n- `StepStatus.FAIL` / `StepStatus.TIMEOUT` ~ `Finding.FAILED` (failure)\n- `StepStatus.SKIPPED` ~ `Finding.SKIPPED` (not executed)\n- `StepStatus.PENDING` ~ `Finding.PENDING` (awaiting execution)\n\nThis alignment ensures conceptual consistency across the
